[30;1m421 | [0m[35m    3) Get operator[0m
[30;1m422 | [0m[35m    4) Use recursion to create tree starting at token on right side of operator (start at step #1)[0m
[30;1m423 | [0m[35m    4.1) If recursive call encounters an operator with lower or equal priority to step #2, exit recu[0m
[30;1m424 | [0m[35m    5) Combine left side, operator, and right side into a new left side[0m
[30;1m425 | [0m[35m    6) Go back to step #2[0m
